I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the ground truth:

**GT: c0*P^(1/3) + c2*P** (where c0 = c2 ≈ 0.101)

The GT is simply a sum of two terms: P^(1/3) and P (with coefficients). There's no dependence on t.

Let me analyze each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `P^0.333*c0 + P*c1` — This is exactly P^(1/3)*c0 + P*c1. Direct match.

= [c0*P^(1/3) + c2*P^2 + (c3+c4)*P + c5*P^(4/3)] / (P+c1)

For this to equal P^(1/3) + aP, we need:
[c0*P^(1/3) + c2*P^2 + (c3+c4)*P + c5*P^(4/3)] / (P+c1) = a*P^(1/3) + b*P

Multiply RHS by (P+c1): a*P^(4/3) + a*c1*P^(1/3) + b*P^2 + b*c1*P

Matching: c2 = b, c5 = a, c0 = a*c1, c3+c4 = b*c1. This is consistent. Set a = c0/c1 (with c1≠0), etc. Match.

= [c0*P^(4/3) + c2*P^(1/3) + c3*P^2 + (c4+c5)*P] / (P+c1)

Need: a*P^(4/3) + a*c1*P^(1/3) + b*P^2 + b*c1*P = c0*P^(4/3) + c2*P^(1/3) + c3*P^2 + (c4+c5)*P
